Economic Community, had granted recognition.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9804acd0"><p class="cl-98045b0e"><span class="cl-98044e20">No</span><span class="cl-98044e20"> </span><span class="cl-980fb774"> </span><span class="cl-980fb774">initiated</span><span class="cl-980fb774"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">unspecified</span><span class="cl-980fb77e"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">cooperation</span><span class="cl-980fb774"> </span><span class="cl-980fb774">toward</span><span class="cl-980fb774"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">Organisation</span><span class="cl-980fb77e"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">of</span><span class="cl-980fb77e"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">African</span><span class="cl-980fb77e"> </span><span class="cl-980fb77e">Unity</span><span class="cl-980fb774">.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
